<script>
	// 底通红包
$(function(){
	var $document = $(document);

	$document.on("click", ".js-footBar-pickup", function(){
			$.ajax({
				 url: 'http://www.lvmama.com/homePage/ajaxGetCouponForBannerActivity.do',
				 dataType: 'json'
			}).done(function (data) {
				 if (data.code == '0') {
					showElevenResultDialog(true,data.bak1,data.bak2);
				 } else if (data.code == '200002') {
					window.location="https://login.lvmama.com/nsso/login?service="+encodeURIComponent(document.location);
				 } else if (data.code == '200003') {
					showElevenResultDialog(false,data.bak1,data.bak2);
                 }
			});
	});

	$document.on("click", ".js-footBar-pickup-rule", function(){
	 	$(".eleven-overlay, .eleven-dialog-rule").show();
	 });

	$document.on("click", ".eleven-dialog .eleven-close", function(){
		$(".eleven-overlay, .eleven-dialog").hide();
	});

	  function showElevenResultDialog(isPickuped,showTime,YORN) {
        var $dialog = $(".eleven-dialog-result");
        var $img = $dialog.find("img");
        var $text = $dialog.find("p.eleven-result-text");
        var $tip = $dialog.find("p.eleven-result-tip");

          if(isPickuped) {
            $img.attr("src", "http://s1.lvjs.com.cn/img/v6/myspace/lv_success.png");
            $text.html("恭喜您领取成功！");
            // 提示
            if(""!=showTime){$tip.html('优惠券使用时间：'+showTime);}
            else if(""!=YORN){$tip.html('<a href="/myspace/account/coupon.do">查看我的优惠券</a>');}
        } else {
            $img.attr("src", "http://s2.lvjs.com.cn/img/v6/myspace/lv_no.png");
            $text.html("抱歉， 您已领取过该大礼包！");
            // 提示
            if(""!=showTime){$tip.html('优惠券使用时间：'+showTime);}
            else if(""!=YORN){$tip.html('<a href="/myspace/account/coupon.do">查看我的优惠券</a>');}
        }
       $(".eleven-dialog-result, .eleven-overlay").show();
    }
    
    if($("#sale_flight_dateTime").val()==''){
    	$("#saleDeptDate").val('2017-10-08');
    }else{
   	 	$("#saleDeptDate").val($("#sale_flight_dateTime").val());
    }
    
    $(".flight_tomorrow").html(getDayOfWeek($("#saleDeptDate").val()));
    $("#sale_flight_days_inner").text("前后"+$("#sale_flight_days").val()+"天");
    
});

//国际机票搜索
    var $ifsSubmit = $(".ifs-submit");
    $ifsSubmit.on("click", function () {
        //验证
        var ret = window.searchSingleton.searchSubmitValidate();
        if (!ret) {
            return;
        }
        var data = $(".ifs-search-form").serialize();
        var searchType = $("input[name='SEARCH_TYPE']:checked").val();
        if (searchType == "multiple") {
            if (ret) {
                var $multiple = $(".ifs-multiple");
                var $items = $multiple.find(".ifs-bm-item");
                var $form = $(".ifs-search-form");

                var cmLog = "首页-PC-"+$("#2017stationName").val()+"-左侧导航-06-机票-国际机票-多程";
                for (var i = 0; i < $items.length; i++) {
                    var $item = $items.eq(i);
                    cmLog += '-行程' + (i + 1);

                    var start = $.trim($item.find(".JS_search_city_start").val());
                    var dest = $.trim($item.find(".JS_search_city_dest").val());
                    var date = $.trim($item.find(".JS_search_multiple_date").val());

                    cmLog += "-" + start + "-" + dest + "-" + date;
                }

                var adult = $form.find(".search-others-adult").find("option:checked").html();
                var child = $form.find(".search-others-child").find("option:checked").html();
                var cabin = $form.find(".search-others-cabin").find("option:checked").html();

                cmLog += "-" + adult + "-" + child + "-" + cabin;
                cmCreateElementTag(cmLog, "PC首页左侧导航")
               	setTimeout(function () {
                    window.location.href = 'http://flight.lvmama.com/international/flight/multiple';
                }, 0);
            }
            return;
        }
        window.location.href = getSearchParam(searchType);
    });

function getSearchParam(searchType) {
    var $searchSingletonFromInput = $("#SEARCH_SINGLE_FORM_ID");
    var $searchSingletonToInput = $("#SEARCH_SINGLE_TO_ID");
    var $searchSingletonFromDate = $(".ifs-bs-from-date .ifs-bs-input");
    var $searchSingletonToDate = $(".ifs-bs-to-date .ifs-bs-input");
    var depart = getSplit($searchSingletonFromInput.val(), "cityCode");
    var arrive = getSplit($searchSingletonToInput.val(), "cityCode");
    var tag = "首页-PC-"+$("#2017stationName").val()+"-左侧导航-06-机票-国际机票";
    var url = 'http://flight.lvmama.com/international/flight/' + depart + "-" + arrive + "?" + $searchSingletonFromDate.val();
    if (searchType != "single") {
        url += "&" + $searchSingletonToDate.val();
        tag += "-往返-"+$("#SEARCH_SINGLE_FORM").val()+ "-" + $("#SEARCH_SINGLE_TO").val() + "-" +$searchSingletonFromDate.val() +"-"+$searchSingletonToDate.val();
    }else{
    	tag += "-单程-"+$("#SEARCH_SINGLE_FORM").val()+ "-" + $("#SEARCH_SINGLE_TO").val() + "-" +$searchSingletonFromDate.val();
    }
    var $form = $(".ifs-search-form");
    var adult = $form.find(".search-others-adult").find("option:checked").html();
    var child = $form.find(".search-others-child").find("option:checked").html();
    var cabin = $form.find(".search-others-cabin").find("option:checked").html();
    tag += "-" + adult + "-" + child + "-" + cabin;
    if ($("#showDirect").prop("checked")) {
        url += "&direct";
		tag += "-直飞";
    }
    cmCreateElementTag(tag, "PC首页左侧导航");
    return url;
}

function getSplit(str, type) {
    var index = 0;
    var typeTable = {"type": 0, "cityCode": 1, "airportCode": 2, "text": 3};
    if (type) {
        index = typeTable[type];
    }
    if (str === "" || str === undefined) {
        return "";
    }
    return str.split("|")[index];
}
 // 搜索特价
$(".ft-sale-btn").on("click", function (e) {
    e.stopPropagation();
    var $this = $(this);
    if (validateFtInput($this)) {
        var deptCity=$("#saleDeptCity").val();
		var arrvCity=$("#saleArrvCity").val();
		var deptDate = $("#saleDeptDate").val();
		var flightDays = $("#sale_flight_days").val();
		$("#sale_flight_days").val(flightDays);
		$("#sale_flight_dateTime").val(deptDate);
		cmCreateElementTag("首页-PC-"+$("#2017stationName").val()+"-左侧导航-06-机票-国内特价-" + deptCity + "-" + arrvCity+"-"+deptDate+"-"+flightDays, "PC首页左侧导航");
		var url = "http://flight.lvmama.com/sale_flight?deptCity="+deptCity+"&arrvCity="+arrvCity+"&deptDate="+deptDate+"&flightDays="+flightDays;
		window.location=url;
    }
});
</script>
